[SELECT_CARRIER](state, { planIds }) {
    state.plans.byId = {
      ...state.plans.allIds.reduce(
        (previousValue, currentPlanId) => ({
          ...previousValue,
          [currentPlanId]: {
            ...state.plans.byId[currentPlanId],
            selected: false,
          },
        }),
        {},
      ),
      ...without([state.plans.allIds], planIds).reduce(
        (previousValue, currentPlanId) => ({
          ...previousValue,
          [currentPlanId]: {
            ...state.plans.byId[currentPlanId],
            selected: true,
          },
        }),
        {},
      ),
    }
    state.plans.selectedIds = planIds
  },
